    <div id="main-content" class="bbs-screen bbs-content"><div class="article-metaline"><span class="article-meta-tag">作者</span><span class="article-meta-value">ioupoiu (他媽的噁心甲)</span></div><div class="article-metaline-right"><span class="article-meta-tag">看板</span><span class="article-meta-value">Gossiping</span></div><div class="article-metaline"><span class="article-meta-tag">標題</span><span class="article-meta-value">[爆卦] 某甲甲輸不起，鼓動腦粉惡意抵制無辜店家</span></div><div class="article-metaline"><span class="article-meta-tag">時間</span><span class="article-meta-value">Mon May 22 21:58:53 2017</span></div>
某PTT紅人參加某店家舉辦的創意影片活動，
結果沒進前三名，就鼓動他的腦粉惡意抵制店家、給1星、洗評價

如下述證據(圖片為保護隱私，大頭貼、ID、店家名稱均打碼)

自己也在洗好意思說人:
<a href="http://i.imgur.com/pODRoGY.jpg" target="_blank" rel="nofollow">http://i.imgur.com/pODRoGY.jpg</a>
<div class="richcontent"><blockquote class="imgur-embed-pub" lang="en" data-id="pODRoGY"><a href="//imgur.com/pODRoGY"></a></blockquote><script async src="//s.imgur.com/min/embed.js" charset="utf-8"></script></div>
輸了就惱羞說店家規則不公平:
<a href="http://i.imgur.com/drNzTSV.jpg" target="_blank" rel="nofollow">http://i.imgur.com/drNzTSV.jpg</a>
<div class="richcontent"><blockquote class="imgur-embed-pub" lang="en" data-id="drNzTSV"><a href="//imgur.com/drNzTSV"></a></blockquote><script async src="//s.imgur.com/min/embed.js" charset="utf-8"></script></div>
事實上店家一開始就有給計算公式:
<a href="http://i.imgur.com/dmLFexM.jpg" target="_blank" rel="nofollow">http://i.imgur.com/dmLFexM.jpg</a>
<div class="richcontent"><blockquote class="imgur-embed-pub" lang="en" data-id="dmLFexM"><a href="//imgur.com/dmLFexM"></a></blockquote><script async src="//s.imgur.com/min/embed.js" charset="utf-8"></script></div>
自己沒有研究好規則，擬定戰略，輸了就說人作弊、不公平，好好笑，
更好笑的是，不爽店家，結果錢還是照拿:
<a href="http://i.imgur.com/IR2fCSC.jpg" target="_blank" rel="nofollow">http://i.imgur.com/IR2fCSC.jpg</a>
<div class="richcontent"><blockquote class="imgur-embed-pub" lang="en" data-id="IR2fCSC"><a href="//imgur.com/IR2fCSC"></a></blockquote><script async src="//s.imgur.com/min/embed.js" charset="utf-8"></script></div>
店家被惡意給1星:
<a href="http://i.imgur.com/Nl2YfCL.jpg" target="_blank" rel="nofollow">http://i.imgur.com/Nl2YfCL.jpg</a>
<div class="richcontent"><blockquote class="imgur-embed-pub" lang="en" data-id="Nl2YfCL"><a href="//imgur.com/Nl2YfCL"></a></blockquote><script async src="//s.imgur.com/min/embed.js" charset="utf-8"></script></div>
大規模、集團式的洗負面評價:
<a href="http://i.imgur.com/dKVSnch.jpg" target="_blank" rel="nofollow">http://i.imgur.com/dKVSnch.jpg</a>
<div class="richcontent"><blockquote class="imgur-embed-pub" lang="en" data-id="dKVSnch"><a href="//imgur.com/dKVSnch"></a></blockquote><script async src="//s.imgur.com/min/embed.js" charset="utf-8"></script></div><a href="http://i.imgur.com/R4Twxfg.jpg" target="_blank" rel="nofollow">http://i.imgur.com/R4Twxfg.jpg</a>
<div class="richcontent"><blockquote class="imgur-embed-pub" lang="en" data-id="R4Twxfg"><a href="//imgur.com/R4Twxfg"></a></blockquote><script async src="//s.imgur.com/min/embed.js" charset="utf-8"></script></div>
這種群眾暴力確實很有效，店家認輸了，多包給這位紅人遺珠獎($5000):
<a href="http://i.imgur.com/X2w481G.jpg" target="_blank" rel="nofollow">http://i.imgur.com/X2w481G.jpg</a>
<div class="richcontent"><blockquote class="imgur-embed-pub" lang="en" data-id="X2w481G"><a href="//imgur.com/X2w481G"></a></blockquote><script async src="//s.imgur.com/min/embed.js" charset="utf-8"></script></div>

這種比賽本來就是比誰會洗、比誰點擊數多，玩不起就別玩阿，
哪有這樣輸了就氣噗噗要抵制？ 自己影片拍得也沒多好.........
你也拿不出確實的證據說人用違法的手段洗票，這樣店家當然無法取消他們的資格
這種號召群眾進行網路霸凌的行為，都不會不好意思？

跟口香糖事件一樣 毫無證據就抹黑

跟麥當勞挑釁事件一樣 發動腦粉


這位PTT紅人票數落後時就汙衊別人作弊的行徑，已不是第一次，
之前參加某活動票數落後時就說人作弊，
還被吐槽說「你們不是也在灌票嗎..還說別人」


被吐槽:
<a href="http://i.imgur.com/F4aCVH2.jpg" target="_blank" rel="nofollow">http://i.imgur.com/F4aCVH2.jpg</a>
<div class="richcontent"><blockquote class="imgur-embed-pub" lang="en" data-id="F4aCVH2"><a href="//imgur.com/F4aCVH2"></a></blockquote><script async src="//s.imgur.com/min/embed.js" charset="utf-8"></script></div>
別人不能朋友很多幫他洗票數？全世界就某PTT紅人你朋友最多喔? 好意思?

超級雙重標準+自助餐的.........


自己贏了卻絕口不提自己也有灌票的行為

自己也在洗票好意思說人:
<a href="http://i.imgur.com/15myXW3.jpg" target="_blank" rel="nofollow">http://i.imgur.com/15myXW3.jpg</a>
<div class="richcontent"><blockquote class="imgur-embed-pub" lang="en" data-id="15myXW3"><a href="//imgur.com/15myXW3"></a></blockquote><script async src="//s.imgur.com/min/embed.js" charset="utf-8"></script></div>
落後就說人灌票:
<a href="http://i.imgur.com/jX0heCb.jpg" target="_blank" rel="nofollow">http://i.imgur.com/jX0heCb.jpg</a>
<div class="richcontent"><blockquote class="imgur-embed-pub" lang="en" data-id="jX0heCb"><a href="//imgur.com/jX0heCb"></a></blockquote><script async src="//s.imgur.com/min/embed.js" charset="utf-8"></script></div>
結果這個某PTT紅人還是拿第一，若別人真是灌票機器人，有可能讓你贏嗎？


看來以後店家辦活動一定要讓某PTT紅人贏~
不然就等著被指控作弊、不公，被抵制吧！

這種____，各大店家自己小心吧....


不然....呵呵.....
